sitedir-ltr mw-hide-empty-elt ns-0 ns-subject page-List_of_states_with_limited_recognition rootpage-List_of_states_with_limited_recognition skin-vector action-view">\t\t<div id="mw-page-base" class="mw-body-content"><!-- CentralNotice --></div><div class="mw-indicators mw-body-content">\n<div id="mw-indicator-pp-default" class="mw-indicator"><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Protection_policy#extended" title="This article is extended-confirmed protected"><img alt="Extended-protected article" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/a/a1/Padlock-blue.svg/20px-Padlock-blue.svg.png" width="20" height="20" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/a/a1/Padlock-blue.svg/30px-Padlock-blue.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/a/a1/Padlock-blue.svg/40px-Padlock-blue.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="128" data-file-height="128" /></a></div>\n</div>\n<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading" lang="en">List of states with limited recognition</h1>\t\t\t<div id="bodyContent" class="mw-body-content">\n\t\t\t\t<div id="siteSub" class="noprint">From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia</div>\t\t\t\t<div id="contentSub"></div>\n\t\t\t\t<div id="jump-to-nav"></div>\t\t\t\t<a class="mw-jump-link" href="#mw-head">Jump to navigation</a>\n\t\t\t\t<a class="mw-jump-link" href="#p-search">Jump to search</a>\n\t\t\t\t<div id="mw-content-text" lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div class="mw-parser-output"><div class="shortdescription nomobile noexcerpt noprint searchaux" style="display:none">Wikimedia list article</div>\n<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">"Disputed states" redirects here. For a list of territorial disputes including these, see <a href="/wiki/List_of_territorial_disputes" title="List of territorial disputes">List of territorial disputes</a>.</div>\n<p class="mw-empty-elt">\n\n</p>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:402px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Limited_recognition.png" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6b/Limited_recognition.png/400px-Limited_recognition.png" width="400" height="212" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6b/Limited_recognition.png/600px-Limited_recognition.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6b/Limited_recognition.png/800px-Limited_recognition.png 2x" data-file-width="1248" data-file-height="660" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Limited_recognition.png" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><div class="legend" style="-webkit-column-break-inside: avoid;page-break-inside: avoid;break-inside: avoid-column"><span class="legend-color" style="display:inline-block; width:1.5em; height:1.5em; margin:1px 0; border:1px solid black; background-color: #808040; color:black; font-size:100%; text-align:center;">&#160;</span>&#160;UN member states which at least one other UN member state does not recognise</div> <div class="legend" style="-webkit-column-break-inside: avoid;page-break-inside: avoid;break-inside: avoid-column"><span class="legend-color" style="display:inline-block; width:1.5em; height:1.5em; margin:1px 0; border:1px solid black; background-color: #FF8040; color:black; font-size:100%; text-align:center;">&#160;</span>&#160;Non-UN member states and observer states recognised by at least one UN member state</div> <div class="legend" style="-webkit-column-break-inside: avoid;page-break-inside: avoid;break-inside: avoid-column"><span class="legend-color" style="display:inline-block; width:1.5em; height:1.5em; margin:1px 0; border:1px solid black; background-color: #FF8484; color:black; font-size:100%; text-align:center;">&#160;</span>&#160;Non-UN member states recognised by other non-UN member states only</div> <div class="legend" style="-webkit-column-break-inside: avoid;page-break-inside: avoid;break-inside: avoid-column"><span class="legend-color" style="display:inline-block; width:1.5em; height:1.5em; margin:1px 0; border:1px solid black; background-color:red; color:black; font-size:100%; text-align:center;">&#160;</span>&#160;Non-UN member state not recognised by any state</div></div></div></div>\n<p>A number of <a href="/wiki/Polity" title="Polity">polities</a> have declared independence and sought <a href="/wiki/Diplomatic_recognition" title="Diplomatic recognition">diplomatic recognition</a> from the <a href="/wiki/International_community" title="International community">international community</a> as <i><a href="/wiki/De_jure" title="De jure">de jure</a></i> <a href="/wiki/Sovereign_state" title="Sovereign state">sovereign states</a>, but have not been universally recognised as such. These entities often have <i><a href="/wiki/De_facto" title="De facto">de facto</a></i> control of their territory. <a href="/wiki/List_of_historical_unrecognized_states" class="mw-redirect" title="List of historical unrecognized states">A number of such entities</a> have existed in the past.\n</p><p>There are two traditional doctrines that provide indicia of how a <i>de jure</i> sovereign state comes into being. The <a href="/wiki/Sovereign_state#Declarative_theory" title="Sovereign state">declarative theory</a> defines a state as a <a href="/wiki/Public_international_law" class="mw-redirect" title="Public international law">person in international law</a> if it meets the following criteria:\n</p>\n<ol><li>a defined territory</li>\n<li>a permanent population</li>\n<li>a government, and</li>\n<li>a capacity to enter into relations with other states.</li></ol>\n<p>According to the declarative theory, an entity\'s statehood is independent of its recognition by other states. By contrast, the <a href="/wiki/Sovereign_state#Constitutive_theory" title="Sovereign state">constitutive theory</a> defines a state as a person of international law only if it is recognised as such by other states that are already a member of the international community.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p><a href="/wiki/Proto-state" title="Proto-state">Proto-states</a> often reference either or both doctrines in order to legitimise their claims to statehood. There are, for example, entities which meet the declarative criteria (with <i><a href="/wiki/De_facto" title="De facto">de facto</a></i> partial or complete control over their claimed territory, a government and a permanent population), but whose statehood is not recognised by any other states. Non-recognition is often a result of conflicts with other countries that claim those entities as integral parts of their territory. In other cases, two or more partially recognised states may claim the same territorial area, with each of them <i>de facto</i> in control of a portion of it (as have been the cases of the <a href="/wiki/Taiwan" title="Taiwan">Republic of China (Taiwan)</a> and the <a href="/wiki/China" title="China">People\'s Republic of China (PRC)</a>, and <a href="/wiki/North_Korea" title="North Korea">North</a> and <a href="/wiki/South_Korea" title="South Korea">South Korea</a>). Entities that are recognised by only a minority of the world\'s states usually reference the declarative doctrine to legitimise their claims.\n</p><p>In many situations, international non-recognition is influenced by the presence of a foreign military force in the territory of the contested entity, making the description of the country\'s <i>de facto</i> status problematic. The international community can judge this military presence too intrusive, reducing the entity to a <a href="/wiki/Puppet_state" title="Puppet state">puppet state</a> where effective <a href="/wiki/Sovereignty" title="Sovereignty">sovereignty</a> is retained by the foreign power. Historical cases in this sense can be seen in <a href="/wiki/Empire_of_Japan" title="Empire of Japan">Japanese</a>-led <a href="/wiki/Manchukuo" title="Manchukuo">Manchukuo</a> or the <a href="/wiki/Nazi_Germany" title="Nazi Germany">German</a>-created <a href="/wiki/Slovak_Republic_(1939%E2%80%931945)" title="Slovak Republic (1939\xe2\x80\x931945)">Slovak Republic</a> and <a href="/wiki/Independent_State_of_Croatia" title="Independent State of Croatia">Independent State of Croatia</a> before and during <a href="/wiki/World_War_II" title="World War II">World War II</a>. In the 1996 case <i><a href="/wiki/Loizidou_v._Turkey" title="Loizidou v. Turkey">Loizidou v. Turkey</a></i>, the <a href="/wiki/European_Court_of_Human_Rights" title="European Court of Human Rights">European Court of Human Rights</a> judged Turkey for having exercised authority in the territory of <a href="/wiki/Northern_Cyprus" title="Northern Cyprus">Northern Cyprus</a>.\n</p><p>There are also entities which do not have control over any territory or do not unequivocally meet the declarative criteria for statehood but have been recognised to exist <i>de jure</i> as sovereign entities by at least one other state. Historically this has happened in the case of the <a href="/wiki/Holy_See" title="Holy See">Holy See</a> (1870\xe2\x80\x931929), <a href="/wiki/Estonia" title="Estonia">Estonia</a>, <a href="/wiki/Latvia" title="Latvia">Latvia</a> and <a href="/wiki/Lithuania" title="Lithuania">Lithuania</a> (during Soviet annexation), and more recently the <a href="/wiki/State_of_Palestine" title="State of Palestine">State of Palestine</a> at the time of its declaration of independence in 1988. The <a href="/wiki/Sovereign_Military_Order_of_Malta" title="Sovereign Military Order of Malta">Sovereign Military Order of Malta</a> is <a href="/wiki/Sovereign_Military_Order_of_Malta#International_status" title="Sovereign Military Order of Malta">currently in this position</a>. See <a href="/wiki/List_of_governments_in_exile" class="mw-redirect" title="List of governments in exile">list of governments in exile</a> for unrecognised governments without control over the territory claimed.\n</p>\n<div id="toc" class="toc"><input type="checkbox" role="button" id="toctogglecheckbox" class="toctogglecheckbox" style="display:none" /><div class="toctitle" lang="en" dir="ltr"><h2>Contents</h2><span class="toctogglespan"><label class="toctogglelabel" for="toctogglecheckbox"></label></span></div>\n<ul>\n<li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-1"><a href="#Criteria_for_inclusion"><span class="tocnumber">1</span> <span class="toctext">Criteria for inclusion</span></a></li>\n<li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-2"><a href="#Background"><span class="tocnumber">2</span> <span class="toctext">Background</span></a></li>\n<li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-3"><a href="#Present_geopolitical_entities_by_level_of_recognition"><span class="tocnumber">3</span> <span class="toctext">Present geopolitical entities by level of recognition</span></a>\n<ul>\n<li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-4"><a href="#UN_member_states_not_recognised_by_at_least_one_UN_member_state"><span class="tocnumber">3.1</span> <span class="toctext">UN member states not recognised by at least one UN member state</span></a></li>\n<li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-5"><a href="#UN_observer_states_not_recognised_by_at_least_one_UN_member_state"><span class="tocnumber">3.2</span> <span class="toctext">UN observer states not recognised by at least one UN member state</span></a></li>\n<li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-6"><a href="#States_that_are_neither_UN_members_nor_UN_observers"><span class="tocnumber">3.3</span> <span class="toctext">States that are neither UN members nor UN observers</span></a></li>\n</ul>\n</li>\n<li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-7"><a href="#Excluded_entities"><span class="tocnumber">4</span> <span class="toctext">Excluded entities</span></a></li>\n<li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-8"><a href="#See_also"><span class="tocnumber">5</span> <span class="toctext">See also</span></a></li>\n<li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-9"><a href="#Notes"><span class="tocnumber">6</span> <span class="toctext">Notes</span></a></li>\n<li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-10"><a href="#References"><span class="tocnumber">7</span> <span class="toctext">References</span></a></li>\n<li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-11"><a href="#Further_reading"><span class="tocnumber">8</span> <span class="toctext">Further reading</span></a></li>\n</ul>\n</div>\n\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Criteria_for_inclusion">Criteria for inclusion</span></h2>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Somaliland_UCID_elections_rally.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2a/Somaliland_UCID_elections_rally.jpg/220px-Somaliland_UCID_elections_rally.jpg" width="220" height="146" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2a/Somaliland_UCID_elections_rally.jpg/330px-Somaliland_UCID_elections_rally.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2a/Somaliland_UCID_elections_rally.jpg/440px-Somaliland_UCID_elections_rally.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1024" data-file-height="680" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Somaliland_UCID_elections_rally.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Women in <a href="/wiki/Somaliland" title="Somaliland">Somaliland</a>, wearing the colors of the Somaliland flag.</div></div></div>\n<p>The criteria for inclusion means a <a href="/wiki/Polity" title="Polity">polity</a> must claim <a href="/wiki/Sovereignty" title="Sovereignty">sovereignty</a>, lack recognition from at least one <a href="/wiki/Member_states_of_the_United_Nations" title="Member states of the United Nations">UN member state</a>, and either:\n</p>\n<ul><li>satisfy the <a href="/wiki/Declarative_theory_of_statehood" class="mw-redirect" title="Declarative theory of statehood">declarative theory of statehood</a>, <i>or</i></li>\n<li>be <a href="/wiki/Diplomatic_recognition" title="Diplomatic recognition">recognised</a> as a state by at least one UN member state.</li></ul>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Background">Background</span></h2>\n<p>There are 193 <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">United Nations</a> (UN) <a href="/wiki/Member_states_of_the_United_Nations" title="Member states of the United Nations">member states</a>, while both the <a href="/wiki/Holy_See" title="Holy See">Holy See</a> and the <a href="/wiki/State_of_Palestine" title="State of Palestine">State of Palestine</a> have <a href="/wiki/United_Nations_General_Assembly_observers" title="United Nations General Assembly observers">observer state status</a> in the United Nations.<sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup> However, some countries fulfill the declarative criteria, are recognised by the large majority of other states and are members of the United Nations, but are still included in the list here because one or more other states do not recognise their statehood, due to territorial claims or other conflicts.\n</p><p>Some states maintain informal (officially non-diplomatic) relations with states that do not officially recognise them. The <a href="/wiki/Republic_of_China" class="mw-redirect" title="Republic of China">Republic of China</a> (Taiwan) is one such state, as it maintains unofficial relations with many other states through its <a href="/wiki/Taipei_Economic_and_Cultural_Representative_Office" title="Taipei Economic and Cultural Representative Office">Economic and Cultural Offices</a>, which allow regular consular services. This allows the ROC to have economic relations even with states that do not formally recognise it. A total of 56 states, including Germany,<sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> Italy,<sup id="cite_ref-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup> the United States,<sup id="cite_ref-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup> and the United Kingdom,<sup id="cite_ref-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup> maintain some form of unofficial mission in the ROC. <a href="/wiki/Kosovo" title="Kosovo">Kosovo</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> the <a href="/wiki/Republic_of_Artsakh" title="Republic of Artsakh">Republic of Artsakh</a> (<a href="/wiki/Nagorno-Karabakh" title="Nagorno-Karabakh">Nagorno-Karabakh</a>),<sup id="cite_ref-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup> the <a href="/wiki/Turkish_Republic_of_Northern_Cyprus" class="mw-redirect" title="Turkish Republic of Northern Cyprus">Turkish Republic of Northern Cyprus</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Abkhazia" title="Abkhazia">Abkhazia</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-AbkhazRepresentation_10-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AbkhazRepresentation-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Transnistria" title="Transnistria">Transnistria</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-AbkhazRepresentation_10-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AbkhazRepresentation-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> the <a href="/wiki/Sahrawi_Republic" class="mw-redirect" title="Sahrawi Republic">Sahrawi Republic</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Somaliland" title="Somaliland">Somaliland</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> and <a href="/wiki/Palestinian_National_Authority" title="Palestinian National Authority">Palestine</a><sup id="cite_ref-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup> also host informal diplomatic missions, and/or maintain special delegations or other informal missions abroad.\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Present_geopolitical_entities_by_level_of_recognition">Present geopolitical entities by level of src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fa/Flag_of_the_People%27s_Republic_of_China.svg/23px-Flag_of_the_People%27s_Republic_of_China.svg.png" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fa/Flag_of_the_People%27s_Republic_of_China.svg/45px-Flag_of_the_People%27s_Republic_of_China.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="900" data-file-height="600" />&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/China" title="China">People\'s Republic of China</a>\n</td>\n<td>1949\n</td>\n<td>The People\'s Republic of China (PRC), proclaimed in 1949, is the more widely recognised of the two claimant governments of "China", the other being the <a href="/wiki/Republic_of_China" class="mw-redirect" title="Republic of China">Republic of China</a> (ROC, also known as Taiwan). The PRC does not accept diplomatic relations with states that recognise the ROC (<a href="/wiki/International_recognition_of_the_Republic_of_China" class="mw-redirect" title="International recognition of the Republic of China">16</a>&#32;UN members and the <a href="/wiki/Holy_See" title="Holy See">Holy See</a> as of&#32;21&#32;August&#32;2018). Most of these states do not officially recognise the PRC as a state, though some states have established relations with the ROC while stating they do not intend to stop recognising the PRC (Kiribati, Nauru).<sup id="cite_ref-29" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-30" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup> Some states which currently recognise only the PRC have attempted simultaneous recognition and relations with the ROC and the PRC in the past (Liberia, Vanuatu).<sup id="cite_ref-31" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-32" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-33" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup> According to <a href="/wiki/United_Nations_General_Assembly_Resolution_2758" title="United Nations General Assembly Resolution 2758">United Nations General Assembly Resolution 2758</a>, the PRC is the only legitimate representative of China to the United Nations.<sup id="cite_ref-China_34-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-China-34">&#91;a&#93;</a></sup>\n</td>\n<td><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/72/Flag_of_the_Republic_of_China.svg/23px-Flag_of_the_Republic_of_China.svg.png" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/72/Flag_of_the_Republic_of_China.svg/35px-Flag_of_the_Republic_of_China.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/72/Flag_of_the_Republic_of_China.svg/45px-Flag_of_the_Republic_of_China.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="900" data-file-height="600" />&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/Taiwan" title="Taiwan">Republic of China</a> claims to be the sole legitimate government over all of <a href="/wiki/Greater_China" title="Greater China">China</a> under the <a href="/wiki/Constitution_of_the_Republic_of_China" title="Constitution of the Republic of China">Constitution of the Republic of China</a>. <div role="note" class="hatnote Israel">31</a> UN members.\n</td>\n<td><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/53/Flag_of_Syria.svg/23px-Flag_of_Syria.svg.png" width="23" height="15" Israel">International recognition</a>\n</td>\n<td style="text-align:center;"><sup id="cite_ref-36" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-36">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-37" id="UN_observer_states_not_recognised_by_at_least_one_UN_member_state">UN observer states not recognised by at least one UN member state</span></h3>\n<table class="wikitable sortable" style="width: 100%">\n\n<tbody><tr>\n<th style="width:12%;">Name\n</th>\n<th style="width:5%;">Declared\n</th>\n<th style="width:38%;">Status\n</th>\n<th style="width:24%;">Other claimants\n</th>\n<th style="width:16%;">Further information\n</th>\n<th style="width:7%;">References\n</th></tr>\n<tr>\n<td><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/00/Flag_of_Palestine.svg/23px-Flag_of_Palestine.svg.png" width="23" height="12" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/00/Flag_of_Palestine.svg/35px-Flag_of_Palestine.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/00/Flag_of_Palestine.svg/46px-Flag_of_Palestine.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1200" data-file-height="600" />&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/State_of_Palestine" title="State of Palestine">State of Palestine</a>\n</td>\n<td>1988\n</td>\n<td>The <a href="/wiki/Palestinian_Liberation_Organization" class="mw-redirect" title="Palestinian Liberation Organization">Palestinian Liberation Organization</a> (PLO) <a href="/wiki/Palestinian_Declaration_of_Independence" title="Palestinian Declaration of Independence">declared</a> the State of Palestine in 1988. At the time the Israeli Armed Forces had control of most of the proclaimed territory.<sup id="cite_ref-saeb_41-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-saeb-41">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup> It is <a href="/wiki/International_recognition_of_the_State_of_Palestine" title="International recognition of the State of Palestine">recognised by&#160;137</a> UN member states, the Holy See,<sup id="cite_ref-42" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-42">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup> and the <a href="/wiki/Sahrawi_Arab_Democratic_Republic" title="Sahrawi Arab Democratic Republic">Sahrawi Arab Democratic Republic</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-43" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-43">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup> Today the PLC (<a href="/wiki/Palestinian_Legislative_Council" title="Palestinian Legislative Council">Palestinian Legislative Council</a>) executes the government functions in all Palestinian territories outside of Israeli military-controlled zones. Prior to the Council\'s administration, the <a href="/wiki/Palestinian_National_Authority" title="Palestinian National Authority">Palestinian National Authority</a> (PNA) was established in 1994 according to the <a href="/wiki/Oslo_Accords" title="Oslo Accords">Oslo Accords</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Israeli-Palestinian_Interim_Agreement" class="mw-redirect" title="Israeli-Palestinian Interim Agreement">Israeli-Palestinian Interim Agreement</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Israel_44-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Israel-44">&#91;b&#93;</a></sup> Palestine participates in the <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">United Nations</a> as <a href="/wiki/United_Nations_General_Assembly_observers#Palestine" title="United Nations General Assembly observers">an observer state</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-45" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-45">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup> and has membership in the <a href="/wiki/Arab_League" title="Arab League">Arab League</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Organisation_of_Islamic_Cooperation" title="Organisation of Islamic Cooperation">Organisation of Islamic Cooperation</a> and <a href="/wiki/UNESCO" title="UNESCO">UNESCO</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-46" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-46">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup> It was accorded non-member observer state status at the United Nations by <a href="/wiki/United_Nations_General_Assembly_resolution_67/19" title="United Nations General Assembly resolution 67/19">United Nations General Assembly resolution 67/19</a>.\n</td>\n<td><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d4/Flag_of_Israel.svg/21px-Flag_of_Israel.svg.png" width="21" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d4/Flag_of_Israel.svg/32px-Flag_of_Israel.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d4/Flag_of_Israel.svg/41px-Flag_of_Israel.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="660" data-file-height="480" />&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/Israel" title="Israel">Israel</a> does not recognise the state of Palestine and controls areas claimed by Palestine.<sup id="cite_ref-Israel_44-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Israel-44">&#91;b&#93;</a></sup> Subject to the ongoing <a href="/wiki/Israeli%E2%80%93Palestinian_peace_process" title="Israeli\xe2\x80\x93Palestinian peace process">Israeli\xe2\x80\x93Palestinian peace process</a>.\n</td>\n<td>Foreign <a href="/wiki/Foreign_relations_of_the_Palestinian_National_Authority" class="mw-redirect" title="Foreign relations of the Palestinian National Authority">relations</a>, missions (<a href="/wiki/List_of_diplomatic_missions_of_Palestine" class="mw-redirect" title="List of diplomatic missions of Palestine">of</a>, <a state">Proposals for a Palestinian state</a>\n</td>\n<td align="center"><sup id="cite_ref-55" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-55">&#91;53&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-56" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-60">&#91;58&#93;</a></sup>\n</td></tr></tbody></table>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="States_that_are_neither_UN_members_nor_UN_observers">States that are neither UN members nor UN observers</span></h3>\n<table class="wikitable sortable" style="width: 100%">\n\n<tbody><tr>\n<th colspan="6">States recognised by at least one UN member state\n</th></tr>\n<tr>\n<th style="width:12%;">Name\n</th>\n<th style="width:5%;">Declared\n</th>\n<th style="width:38%;">Status\n</th>\n<th style="width:24%;">Other claimants\n</th>\n<th style="width:16%;">Further information\n</th>\n<th style="width:7%;">References\n</th></tr>\n<tr>\n<td><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1f/Flag_of_Kosovo.svg/21px-Flag_of_Kosovo.svg.png" width="21" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1f/Flag_of_Kosovo.svg/32px-Flag_of_Kosovo.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1f/Flag_of_Kosovo.svg/42px-Flag_of_Kosovo.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="840" data-file-height="600" />&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/Kosovo" title="Kosovo">Republic of Kosovo</a>\n</td>\n<td>2008\n</td>\n<td>Kosovo declared its independence in 2008. It is currently recognised by <a href="/wiki/International_recognition_of_Kosovo#Member_states_of_the_United_Nations" title="International recognition of Kosovo">111</a> UN members, the <a href="/wiki/Republic_of_China" class="mw-redirect" title="Republic of China">Republic of China</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Cook_Islands" title="Cook Islands">Cook Islands</a>, <a href="/wiki/Niue" title="Niue">Niue</a>, and the <a href="/wiki/Sovereign_Military_Order_of_Malta" title="Sovereign Military Order of Malta">Sovereign Military Order of Malta</a>. Two other UN members (<a href="/wiki/Burundi" title="Burundi">Burundi</a> and <a href="/wiki/Suriname" title="Suriname">Suriname</a>) have recognised Kosovo and subsequently withdrawn recognition. The <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">United Nations</a>, as stipulated in <a href="/wiki/United_Nations_Security_Council_Resolution_1244" title="United Nations Security Council Resolution 1244">Security Council Resolution 1244</a>, has administered the territory since 1999 through the <a href="/wiki/United_Nations_Interim_Administration_Mission_in_Kosovo" title="United Nations Interim Administration Mission in Kosovo">United Nations Interim Administration Mission in Kosovo</a>, with cooperation from the <a href="/wiki/European_Union_Rule_of_Law_Mission_in_Kosovo" title="European Union Rule of Law Mission in Kosovo">European Union</a> since 2008. It is a member of the <a href="/wiki/International_Monetary_Fund" title="International Monetary Fund">International Monetary Fund</a>, <a href="/wiki/World_Bank_Group" title="World Bank Group">World Bank Group</a>, <a href="/wiki/Venice_Commission" title="Venice Commission">Venice Commission</a>, <a href="/wiki/European_Bank_for_Reconstruction_and_Development" title="European Bank for Reconstruction and Development">European Bank for Reconstruction and Development</a>, and the <a href="/wiki/International_Olympic_Committee" title="International Olympic Committee">International Olympic Committee</a>, among others.\n</td>\n<td><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/ff/Flag_of_Serbia.svg/23px-Flag_of_Serbia.svg.png" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/ff/Flag_of_Serbia.svg/35px-Flag_of_Serbia.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/ff/Flag_of_Serbia.svg/45px-Flag_of_Serbia.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="945" data-file-height="630" />&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/Serbia" title="Serbia">Serbia</a> claims Kosovo as part of its sovereign territory.\n</td>\n<td>Foreign <a href="/wiki/Foreign_relations_of_Kosovo" title="Foreign relations of Kosovo">relations</a>, missions (<a href="/wiki/List_of_diplomatic_missions_of_Kosovo" title="List of diplomatic missions of Kosovo">of</a>, <a href="/wiki/List_of_diplomatic_missions_in_Kosovo" title="List of diplomatic missions in Kosovo">to</a>)<hr /> <a href="/wiki/International_recognition_of_Kosovo" title="International recognition of Kosovo">International recognition</a>; <a href="/wiki/Political_status_of_Kosovo" title="Political status of Kosovo">Political status</a>\n</td>\n<td align="center"><sup id="cite_ref-61" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-61">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-62" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-62">&#91;60&#93;</a></sup>\n</td></tr>\n<tr>\n<td><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/26/Flag_of_the_Sahrawi_Arab_Democratic_Republic.svg/23px-Flag_of_the_Sahrawi_Arab_Democratic_Republic.svg.png" width="23" height="12" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/26/Flag_of_the_Sahrawi_Arab_Democratic_Republic.svg/35px-Flag_of_the_Sahrawi_Arab_Democratic_Republic.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/26/Flag_of_the_Sahrawi_Arab_Democratic_Republic.svg/46px-Flag_of_the_Sahrawi_Arab_Democratic_Republic.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="600" data-file-height="300" />&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/Sahrawi_Arab_Democratic_Republic" title="Sahrawi Arab Democratic Republic">Sahrawi Arab Democratic Republic</a>\n</td>\n<td>1976\n</td>\n<td>Both the Sahrawi Arab Democratic Republic (SADR) and <a href="/wiki/Morocco" title="Morocco">Morocco</a> claim sovereignty over the territory of <a href="/wiki/Western_Sahara" title="Western Sahara">Western Sahara</a>. The SADR, which declared its independence in 1976, is currently recognised by <a href="/wiki/International_recognition_of_the_Sahrawi_Arab_Democratic_Republic#States_that_have_recognized_SADR" title="International recognition of the Sahrawi Arab Democratic Republic">46</a> UN member states and <a href="/wiki/South_Ossetia" title="South Ossetia">South Ossetia</a>. 38 other UN member states have recognised the SADR but subsequently retracted or suspended recognition, pending the outcome of a <a href="/wiki/Referendum" title="Referendum">referendum</a> on <a href="/wiki/Self-determination" title="Self-determination">self-determination</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-63" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-63">&#91;61&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-64" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-64">&#91;62&#93;</a></sup> Western Sahara is not recognised as part of Morocco by any state, but some states support the <a href="/wiki/Moroccan_Initiative_for_Western_Sahara" class="mw-redirect" title="Moroccan Initiative for Western Sahara">Moroccan autonomy plan</a>. Moroccan "territorial integrity" is favoured by the <a href="/wiki/Arab_League" title="Arab League">Arab League</a>. The SADR is a member of the <a href="/wiki/African_Union" title="African Union">African Union</a>. United Nations General Assembly Resolution 34/37 recognised the right of the Western Sahara people to self-determination and recognised also the Polisario Front as the representative of the Western Sahara people.<sup id="cite_ref-65" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-65">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup> Western Sahara is listed on the <a href="/wiki/United_Nations_list_of_Non-Self-Governing_Territories" title="United Nations list of Non-Self-Governing Territories">United Nations list of Non-Self-Governing Territories</a>.\n</td>\n<td><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2c/Flag_of_Morocco.svg/23px-Flag_of_Morocco.svg.png" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2c/Flag_of_Morocco.svg/35px-Flag_of_Morocco.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2c/Flag_of_Morocco.svg/45px-Flag_of_Morocco.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="900" data-file-height="600" />&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/Morocco" title="Morocco">Morocco</a> claims Western Sahara as part of its sovereign territory.\n</td>\n<td>Foreign <a href="/wiki/Foreign_relations_of_the_Sahrawi_Arab_Democratic_Republic" title="Foreign relations of the Sahrawi Arab Democratic Republic">relations</a>, missions (<a href="/wiki/List_of_diplomatic_missions_of_Sahrawi_Republic" class="mw-redirect" title="List of diplomatic missions of Sahrawi Republic">of</a>, <a href="/wiki/List_of_diplomatic_missions_in_Sahrawi_Republic" class="mw-redirect" title="List of diplomatic missions in Sahrawi Republic">to</a>)<hr /> <a href="/wiki/International_recognition_of_the_Sahrawi_Arab_Democratic_Republic" title="International recognition of the Sahrawi Arab Democratic Republic">International recognition</a>; <a href="/wiki/Political_status_of_Western_Sahara" title="Political status of Western Sahara">Political status</a>\n</td>\n<td align="center"><sup id="cite_ref-66" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-66">&#91;64&#93;</a></sup>\n</td></tr>\n<tr>\n<td><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/72/Flag_of_the_Republic_of_China.svg/23px-Flag_of_the_Republic_of_China.svg.png" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/72/Flag_of_the_Republic_of_China.svg/35px-Flag_of_the_Republic_of_China.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/72/Flag_of_the_Republic_of_China.svg/45px-Flag_of_the_Republic_of_China.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="900" data-file-height="600" />&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/Taiwan" title="Taiwan">Republic of China</a>\n</td>\n<td>1912<sup id="cite_ref-67" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-67">&#91;c&#93;</a></sup>\n</td>\n<td>The Republic of China (ROC, usually called Taiwan), constitutionally formed in 1912, enjoyed majority recognition as the sole government of China until the end of the <a href="/wiki/Chinese_Civil_War" title="Chinese Civil War">Chinese Civil War</a>, after which a majority of UN member states have gradually switched recognition to the <a href="/wiki/People%27s_Republic_of_China" class="mw-redirect" title="People&#39;s Republic of China">People\'s Republic of China</a>. The ROC is currently recognised as a state by <a href="/wiki/International_recognition_of_the_Republic_of_China" class="mw-redirect" title="International recognition of the Republic of China">16</a> UN members and the <a href="/wiki/Holy_See" title="Holy See">Holy See</a>. The remaining UN member states either regard its controlled territory as <i>de jure</i> part of the <a href="/wiki/China" title="China">People\'s Republic of China</a> (PRC) or have used careful diplomatic language to avoid taking a position as to whether the territory of the ROC is part of the PRC.<sup id="cite_ref-China_34-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-China-34">&#91;a&#93;</a></sup> Throughout the years, the ROC has adopted differing positions towards simultaneous recognition of the ROC and the PRC by other countries.<sup id="cite_ref-69" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-69">&#91;66&#93;</a></sup>\n</td>\n<td><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fa/Flag_of_the_People%27s_Republic_of_China.svg/23px-Flag_of_the_People%27s_Republic_of_China.svg.png" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fa/Flag_of_the_People%27s_Republic_of_China.svg/35px-Flag_of_the_People%27s_Republic_of_China.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fa/Flag_of_the_People%27s_Republic_of_China.svg/45px-Flag_of_the_People%27s_Republic_of_China.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="900" data-file-height="600" />&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/China" title="China">People\'s Republic of China</a> claims to be the successor of the former <a href="/wiki/Republic_of_China_(1912-1949)" class="mw-redirect" title="Republic of China (1912-1949)">Republic of China</a> and claims all of the <a href="/wiki/Free_area_of_the_Republic_of_China" title="Free area of the Republic of China">territory under ROC jurisdiction</a> as part of its sovereign territory. <div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/Two_Chinas" title="Two Chinas">Two href="/wiki/Nagorno-Karabakh" title="Nagorno-Karabakh">Nagorno-Karabakh</a>) and <a href="/wiki/Transnistria" title="Transnistria">Transnistria</a>).<sup id="cite_ref-tiraspoltimes.com_71-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-tiraspoltimes.com-71">&#91;68&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-NKRrecognition_72-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-NKRrecognition-72">&#91;69&#93;</a></sup> />&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/Abkhazia" title="Abkhazia">Republic of Abkhazia</a>\n</td>\n<td>1999\n</td>\n<td>Abkhazia declared its independence in 1999.<sup id="cite_ref-78" class="reference"><a <a href="/wiki/Nauru" title="Nauru">Nauru</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Syria" title="Syria">Syria</a>), and three UN non-member states (<a href="/wiki/South_Ossetia" title="South Ossetia">South Ossetia</a>, <a href="/wiki/Transnistria" title="Transnistria">Transnistria</a> and <a href="/wiki/Republic_of_Artsakh" title="Republic of Artsakh">Republic of Artsakh</a>).<sup id="cite_ref-tiraspoltimes.com_71-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-tiraspoltimes.com-71">&#91;68&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-79" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-79">&#91;76&#93;</a></sup> Two other UN member states (<a href="/wiki/Tuvalu" title="Tuvalu">Tuvalu</a> and <a href="/wiki/Vanuatu" title="Vanuatu">Vanuatu</a>) have recognised Abkhazia<sup id="cite_ref-80" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-80">&#91;77&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-81" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-81">&#91;78&#93;</a></sup><sup data-file-height="684" />&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/Northern_Cyprus" title="Northern Cyprus">Turkish Republic of Northern Cyprus</a>\n</td>\n<td>1983\n</td>\n<td>Northern Cyprus declared its independence in 1983. It is recognised by one UN member, <a href="/wiki/Turkey" title="Turkey">Turkey</a>. The <a href="/wiki/Organisation_of_Islamic_Cooperation" title="Organisation of Islamic Cooperation">Organisation of Islamic Cooperation</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Economic_Cooperation_Organization" title="Economic Cooperation Organization">Economic Cooperation Organization</a> have granted Northern Cyprus observer status under the name "Turkish Cypriot State". <a href="/wiki/United_Nations_Security_Council_Resolution_541" title="United Nations Security Council Resolution 541">United Nations Security Council Resolution 541</a> defines the declaration of independence of Northern Cyprus as legally invalid.<sup id="cite_ref-88" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-88">&#91;85&#93;</a></sup> The <a href="/wiki/International_Court_of_Justice" title="International Court of Justice">International Court of Justice</a> stated <a href="/wiki/International_Court_of_Justice_advisory_opinion_on_Kosovo%27s_declaration_of_independence" title="International Court of Justice advisory opinion on Kosovo&#39;s declaration of independence">in its advisory opinion on Kosovo\'s declaration of independence in 2010</a> that "the Security Council in an exceptional character attached illegality to the DOI of TRNC because it was, or would have been connected with the unlawful use of force" and "general international law contains no applicable prohibition of declarations of independence".<sup id="cite_ref-International_Court_of_Justice_89-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-International_Court_of_Justice-89">&#91;86&#93;</a></sup>\n</td>\n<td><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d4/Flag_of_Cyprus.svg/23px-Flag_of_Cyprus.svg.png" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d4/Flag_of_Cyprus.svg/35px-Flag_of_Cyprus.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d4/Flag_of_Cyprus.svg/45px-Flag_of_Cyprus.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="900" data-file-height="600" />&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/Cyprus" title="Cyprus">Cyprus</a> claims Northern Cyprus as part of its sovereign territory.\n</td>\n<td>Foreign <a href="/wiki/Foreign_relations_of_the_Turkish_Republic_of_Northern_Cyprus" class="mw-redirect" title="Foreign relations of the Turkish Republic of Northern Cyprus">relations</a>, missions (<a href="/wiki/List_of_diplomatic_missions_of_Northern_Cyprus" title="List of diplomatic missions of Northern Cyprus">of</a>, <a href="/wiki/List_of_diplomatic_missions_in_Northern_Cyprus" title="List of diplomatic missions in Northern Cyprus">to</a>)<hr /> <a width="23" height="12" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4d/Flag_of_Somaliland.svg/35px-Flag_of_Somaliland.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4d/Flag_of_Somaliland.svg/46px-Flag_of_Somaliland.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1200" data-file-height="600" />&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/Somaliland" title="Somaliland">Republic of Somaliland</a>\n</td>\n<td>1991\n</td>\n<td>Somaliland declared its independence from Somalia in 1991. It claims to be the successor to the <a href="/wiki/State_of_Somaliland" title="State of Somaliland">State of Somaliland</a>, a short lived sovereign state that existed from 26 June 1960 (when the <a href="/wiki/British_Somaliland_Protectorate" class="mw-redirect" title="British Somaliland Protectorate">British Somaliland Protectorate</a> gained full independence from the United Kingdom) to 1 July 1960 (when the State of Somaliland united with Somalia to form the <a href="/wiki/Somali_Republic" title="Somali Republic">Somali Republic</a>). Somaliland is internationally recognised as an <a href="/wiki/States_and_regions_of_Somalia" title="States and regions of Somalia">autonomous region</a> of <a href="/wiki/Somalia" title="Somalia">Somalia</a>.\n</td>\n<td><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a0/Flag_of_Somalia.svg/23px-Flag_of_Somalia.svg.png" width="23" href="/wiki/List_of_diplomatic_missions_in_Somaliland" title="List of diplomatic missions in Somaliland">to</a>)\n</td>\n<td style="text-align:center;"><sup id="cite_ref-montevideo_91-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-montevideo-91">&#91;88&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-94" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-94">&#91;91&#93;</a></sup>\n</td></tr></tbody></table>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Excluded_entities">Excluded entities</span></h2>\n<ul><li>The <span id="Sovereign_Military_Order_of_Malta"></span><a href="/wiki/Sovereign_Military_Order_of_Malta" title="Sovereign Military Order of Malta">Sovereign Military Order of Malta</a> is a non-state <a href="/wiki/Sovereignty" title="Sovereignty">sovereign</a> entity and is not included, as it claims neither statehood nor territory.<sup id="cite_ref-95" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-95">&#91;92&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-96" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-96">&#91;93&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-97" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-97">&#91;94&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-98" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-98">&#91;95&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-99" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-99">&#91;96&#93;</a></sup> It has established full <a href="/wiki/Foreign_relations_of_the_Sovereign_Military_Order_of_Malta" title="Foreign relations of the Sovereign Military Order of Malta">diplomatic relations with 105</a> sovereign states <a href="/wiki/Sovereign_Military_Order_of_Malta#International_status_of_the_Order" title="Sovereign Military Order of Malta">as a sovereign subject of international law</a><sup id="cite_ref-100" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-100">&#91;97&#93;</a></sup> and participates in the United Nations as an <a href="/wiki/United_Nations_General_Assembly_observers#Other_entities" title="United Nations General Assembly observers">observer entity</a>. Although it is not recognised as a subject of international law by <a href="/wiki/France" title="France">France</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-101" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-101">&#91;98&#93;</a></sup> the order maintains official, but not diplomatic, relations with France and also with five other states: <a href="/wiki/Germany" title="Germany">Germany</a>, <a href="/wiki/Belgium" title="Belgium">Belgium</a>, <a href="/wiki/Switzerland" title="Switzerland">Switzerland</a>, <a href="/wiki/Luxembourg" title="Luxembourg">Luxembourg</a> and <a href="/wiki/Canada" title="Canada">Canada</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-102" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-102">&#91;99&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-103" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-103">&#91;100&#93;</a></sup></li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/Uncontacted_peoples" title="Uncontacted peoples">Uncontacted peoples</a> who either live in <a href="/wiki/Stateless_society" title="Stateless society">societies that cannot be defined as states</a> or whose statuses as such are not definitively known.</li>\n<li>Entities considered to be <a href="/wiki/Micronation" title="Micronation">micronations</a> are not included.<sup id="cite_ref-Micronation1_104-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Micronation1-104">&#91;d&#93;</a></sup>  Even though micronations generally claim to be sovereign and independent, it is often debatable whether a micronation truly controls its claimed territory.<sup id="cite_ref-Micronation2_105-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Micronation2-105">&#91;e&#93;</a></sup> For this reason, micronations are usually not considered of geopolitical relevance. For a list of micronations, see <a href="/wiki/List_of_micronations" title="List of micronations">list of micronations</a>.</li>\n<li>Those areas undergoing current <a href="/wiki/List_of_civil_wars" title="List of civil wars">civil wars</a> and other situations with problems over government succession, regardless of temporary alignment with <a href="#Criteria_for_inclusion">the inclusion criteria</a> (e.g. by receiving recognition as state or legitimate government), where the conflict is still in its active phase, the situation is too rapidly changing and no relatively stable <a href="/wiki/List_of_rump_states" class="mw-redirect" title="List of rump states">rump states</a> have emerged yet.</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/Rebel_groups" class="mw-redirect" title="Rebel groups">Rebel groups</a> that have <a href="/wiki/Declaration_of_independence" title="Declaration of independence">declared independence</a> and exert some <a href="/wiki/Territorial_entity" title="Territorial entity">control over territory</a>, but that reliable sources do not describe as meeting the threshold of a sovereign state under international law. Examples include <a href="/wiki/Donetsk_People%27s_Republic" title="Donetsk People&#39;s Republic">Donetsk People\'s Republic</a>, <a href="/wiki/Luhansk_People%27s_Republic" title="Luhansk People&#39;s Republic">Luhansk People\'s Republic</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Islamic_State_of_Iraq_and_the_Levant" title="Islamic State of Iraq and the Levant">Islamic State of Iraq and the Levant</a> (see <a href="/wiki/List_of_rebel_groups_that_control_territory" class="mw-redirect" title="List of rebel groups that control territory">List of rebel groups that control territory</a> for a more complete list of such groups).</li>\n<li>Those of the current <a href="/wiki/Irredentist_movements" class="mw-redirect" title="Irredentist movements">irredentist movements</a> and <a href="/wiki/Government_in_exile#Current_governments_in_exile" title="Government in exile">governments in exile</a> that do not satisfy <a href="#Criteria_for_inclusion">the inclusion criteria</a> by simultaneously not satisfying the declarative theory and not having been recognised as state or legitimate government by any other state.</li>\n<li>Some states can be slow to establish relations with new UN member states and thus do not recognise them, despite having no dispute and sometimes favorable relations. These are excluded from the list.</li></ul>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="See_also">See also</span></h2>\n<div role="navigation" aria-label="Portals" class="noprint portal plainlist tright" Organization</a></li></ul>\n</div>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Notes">Notes</span></h2>\n<div class="reflist columns references-column-width" style="-moz-column-width: 30em; -webkit-column-width: 30em; column-width: 30em; list-style-type: lower-alpha;">\n<ol class="references">\n<li id="cite_note-China-34"><span class="mw-cite-backlink">^ <a href="#cite_ref-China_34-0"><sup><i><b>a</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-China_34-1"><sup><i><b>b</b></i></sup></a></span> <span class="reference-text">Both the Republic of China and the People\'s Republic of China <a href="/wiki/1992_Consensus" title="1992 Consensus">claim sovereignty over the whole of China</a>, stating <a href="/wiki/Greater_China" title="Greater China">China</a> is <i>de jure</i> a single sovereign entity encompassing both the area controlled by the PRC and the area controlled by the ROC. The position of individual states on this matter varies. Several states fully accept the PRC\'s position that there is only one China and that the PRC is the sole legitimate representative of China. Other states merely acknowledge this position, while recognising only the PRC as a state. Some states recognise only the ROC as a state, but have expressed an interest in recognition and relations with both the ROC and the PRC.<sup id="cite_ref-68" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-68">&#91;65&#93;</a></sup></span>\n</li>\n<li id="cite_note-Israel-44"><span class="mw-cite-backlink">^ <a href="#cite_ref-Israel_44-0"><sup><i><b>a</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-Israel_44-1"><sup><i><b>b</b></i></sup></a></span> <span class="reference-text">Israel allows the PNA to execute some functions in the <a href="/wiki/Palestinian_territories" title="Palestinian territories">Palestinian territories</a>, depending on <a href="/wiki/Administrative_divisions_of_the_Oslo_Accords" class="mw-redirect" title="Administrative divisions of the Oslo Accords">special area classification</a>. Israel maintains <a href="/wiki/Israel%27s_unilateral_disengagement_plan" class="mw-redirect" title="Israel&#39;s unilateral disengagement plan">minimal interference</a> (retaining control of borders: <a href="/wiki/National_airspace" class="mw-redirect" title="National airspace">air</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-GazaSeaAir_47-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GazaSeaAir-47">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup> sea <a href="/wiki/Third_United_Nations_Convention_on_the_Law_of_the_Sea" class="mw-redirect" title="Third United Nations Convention on the Law of the Sea">beyond internal waters</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-GazaSeaAir_47-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GazaSeaAir-47">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-48" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-48">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/European_Union_Border_Assistance_Mission_Rafah" class="mw-redirect" title="European Union Border Assistance Mission Rafah">land</a><sup id="cite_ref-49" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-49">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup>) in the <a href="/wiki/Gaza_strip" class="mw-redirect" title="Gaza strip">Gaza strip</a> (its interior and Egypt portion of the land border are under <a href="/wiki/Governance_of_the_Gaza_Strip" title="Governance of the Gaza Strip">Hamas control</a>), maximum in "<a href="/wiki/Area_C_(West_Bank)" title="Area C (West Bank)">Area C</a>" and varying degrees of interference elsewhere.<sup id="cite_ref-DoreGold_50-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DoreGold-50">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-AbrahamBell_51-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AbrahamBell-51">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-HerzliyaCon_52-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HerzliyaCon-52">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-ZakSalih_53-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ZakSalih-53">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-IsDisengagement_54-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-IsDisengagement-54">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup> See also <a href="/wiki/Israeli-occupied_territories" title="Israeli-occupied territories">Israeli-occupied territories</a>.<br /><sup id="cite_ref-saeb_41-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-saeb-41">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-DoreGold_50-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DoreGold-50">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-AbrahamBell_51-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AbrahamBell-51">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-HerzliyaCon_52-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HerzliyaCon-52">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-ZakSalih_53-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ZakSalih-53">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-IsDisengagement_54-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-IsDisengagement-54">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup> </span>\n</li>\n<li id="cite_note-67"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-67">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Date of constitutional formation.</span>\n</li>\n<li id="cite_note-Micronation1-104"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-Micronation1_104-0">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Micronations are not included even if they are recognised by another micronation</span>\n</li>\n<li id="cite_note-Micronation2-105"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-Micronation2_105-0">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">It is far from certain that micronations, which are generally of minuscule size, have sovereign control over their claimed territories, contrasted with the mere disregard and indifference toward micronations\xe2\x80\x99 assertions by the states from which they allege to have seceded. By not deeming such declarations (and other acts of the micronation) important enough to react in any way, these states generally consider micronations to be private property and their claims as unofficial private announcements of individuals, who remain subject to the laws of the states in which their properties are located.</span>\n</li>\n</ol></div>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="References">References</span></h2>\n<div class="reflist columns references-column-width" style="-moz-column-width: 30em; -webkit-column-width: 30em; column-width: 30em; list-style-type: decimal;">\n<ol class="references">\n<li id="cite_note-1"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-1">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Thomas D. Retrieved <span class="nowrap">1 August</span> 2015</span>.</cite><span title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook&amp;rft.genre=unknown&amp;rft.btitle=La+Orden+de+Malta+y+su+Naturaleza+Jur%C3%ADdica&amp;rft.pub=%27%27Venezuela+Analitica%27%27&amp;rft.date=1999-05-01&amp;rft_id=http%3A%2F%2Fanalitica.com%2Fopinion%2Fopinion-nacional%2Fla-orden-de-malta-y-su-naturaleza-juridica%2F&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fen.wikipedia.org%3AList+of+states+with+limited+recognition" class="Z3988"></span><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r861714446"/> <a href="/wiki/Talk:Sovereign_Military_Order_of_Malta#&quot;La_Orden_de_Malta_y_su_Naturaleza_Jur\xc3\xaddica&quot;_(English_translation)_-_detailed,_expert_perspective" title="Talk:Sovereign Military Order of Malta">English language translation</a> "The Order of Malta, within the limits that are compatible with its actual position as a subject deprived of territory, is in the international community, a sovereign entity on par with the States, and the Prince Grand Master is comparable, from the point of view of international law, to the Heads of State."</span>\n</li>\n<li id="cite_note-96"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-96">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://web.archive.org/web/20110806055657/http://www.un.int/orderofmalta/orderandun.html">Permanent Observer Mission of the Order of Malta to the United Nations in New York</a> "The admission of Order of Malta to the United Nations also further solidified its legally recognized sovereignty ..."</span>\n</li>\n<li id="cite_note-97"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-97">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Shaw, Malcolm Nathan <i>International Law</i> Fifth Edition Cambridge University Press 2003 <a href="/wiki/International_Standard_Book_Number" title="International Standard Book Number">ISBN</a>&#160;<a href="/wiki/Special:BookSources/0-521-82473-7" title="Special:BookSources/0-521-82473-7">0-521-82473-7</a> p. 218 <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.amazon.com/International-Law-Malcolm-N-Shaw/dp/0521824737/ref=sr_1_1?s=books&amp;ie=UTF8&amp;qid=1351263623&amp;sr=1-1&amp;keywords=0521824737">Searchable text</a>, available via <a href="/wiki/Amazon.com" class="mw-redirect" title="Amazon.com">Amazon.com</a>, "The Italian Court of Cassation in 1935 recognised the international personality of the Order, noting that \xe2\x80\x98the modern theory of the subjects of international law recognises a number of collective units whose composition is independent of the nationality of their constituent members and whose scope transcends by virtue of their universal character the territorial confines of any single state.\xe2\x80\x99 (<i>Nanni v. Pace and the Sovereign Order of Malta</i> 8 AD, p. 2. See also \xe2\x80\xa6)"</span>\n</li>\n<li id="cite_note-98"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-98">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><cite class="citation news"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://drive.google.com/file/d/0B9LDb9lFYjVPMkNwdTBGeVk1T3c/view">"Recon\xc3\xb3cese a la Soberana Orden Militar de Malta como Entidad Internacion\xc3\xa1l Independiente"</a>. <i>Bolet\xc3\xadn Ofici\xc3\xa1l de la Rep\xc3\xbablica Argentina, A\xc3\xb1o LIX, N\xc3\xbamero 16.92</i>. Buenos Aires. 19 June 1951. p.&#160;1.</cite><span title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Ajournal&amp;rft.genre=article&amp;rft.jtitle=Bolet%C3%ADn+Ofici%C3%A1l+de+la+Rep%C3%BAblica+Argentina%2C+A%C3%B1o+LIX%2C+N%C3%BAmero+16.92&amp;rft.atitle=Recon%C3%B3cese+a+la+Soberana+Orden+Militar+de+Malta+como+Entidad+Internacion%C3%A1l+Independiente&amp;rft.pages=1&amp;rft.date=1951-06-19&amp;rft_id=https%3A%2F%2Fdrive.google.com%2Ffile%2Fd%2F0B9LDb9lFYjVPMkNwdTBGeVk1T3c%2Fview&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fen.wikipedia.org%3AList+of+states+with+limited+recognition" class="Z3988"></span><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r861714446"/> "The Senate and Chamber of Deputies of Argentina, in Congress assembled, enact as LAW: Article 1 \xe2\x80\x93 The Sovereign Military Order of Malta is hereby recognized as an international independent entity."</span>\n</li>\n<li id="cite_note-99"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-99">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><cite class="citation web"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://analitica.com/opinion/opinion-nacional/la-orden-de-malta-y-su-naturaleza-juridica/">"La Orden de Malta y su Naturaleza Jur\xc3\xaddica"</a>. <i><a href="/wiki/Venezuela_Analitica" title="Venezuela Analitica">Venezuela Analitica</a></i>. 1 May 1999. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://web.archive.org/web/20150801044650/http://analitica.com/opinion/opinion-nacional/la-orden-de-malta-y-su-naturaleza-juridica/">Archived</a> from the original on 1 August 2015<span class="reference-accessdate">. Retrieved <span class="nowrap">1 August</span> 2015</span>.</cite><span title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook&amp;rft.genre=unknown&amp;rft.btitle=La+Orden+de+Malta+y+su+Naturaleza+Jur%C3%ADdica&amp;rft.pub=%27%27Venezuela+Analitica%27%27&amp;rft.date=1999-05-01&amp;rft_id=http%3A%2F%2Fanalitica.com%2Fopinion%2Fopinion-nacional%2Fla-orden-de-malta-y-su-naturaleza-juridica%2F&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fen.wikipedia.org%3AList+of+states+with+limited+recognition" class="Z3988"></span><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r861714446"/> <a href="/wiki/Talk:Sovereign_Military_Order_of_Malta#&quot;La_Orden_de_Malta_y_su_Naturaleza_Jur\xc3\xaddica&quot;_(English_translation)_-_detailed,_expert_perspective" title="Talk:Sovereign Military Order of Malta">English language translation</a> "[T]he clear territorial separation of sovereign areas that exists between the Italian State and the State of Vatican City does not exist between the Order of Malta and the Italian State, but neither can it be said that the treatment given to the headquarters of the Order (Aventine, Via Condotti) is, simply, that reserved for the headquarters of diplomatic missions accredited to the Italian State. In fact, the headquarters of the Order have diplomatic extraterritoriality (authoritarian acts of any kind \xe2\x80\x93 executive, acts of inspection, judicial \xe2\x80\x93 cannot take place inside), but in addition, the Italian State recognizes the exercise, in the headquarters, of the prerogatives of sovereignty. This means that Italian sovereignty and Maltese sovereignty coexist without overlapping, because the Order exercises sovereign functions in a wider area than occurs in the diplomatic missions of the States for, although [those diplomatic missions] enjoy extraterritoriality, the guarantees deriving from the privilege of immunity are constrained to a purely administrative area; the Order, instead, makes use of extraterritoriality to meet the very acts of sovereign self-determination that are the same as the States (legislative, judicial, administrative, financial acts)."</span>\n</li>\n<li id="cite_note-100"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-100">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">The Sovereign Military Order of Malta maintains <a href="/wiki/List_of_diplomatic_missions_of_the_Sovereign_Military_Order_of_Malta" title="List of diplomatic missions of the Sovereign Military Order of Malta">embassies around the world</a> and receives <a href="/wiki/List_of_diplomatic_missions_to_the_Sovereign_Military_Order_of_Malta" title="List of diplomatic missions to the Sovereign Military Order of Malta">accreditations from foreign ambassadors</a>.</span>\n</li>\n<li id="cite_note-101"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-101">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text"><cite class="citation web"><a class="Z3988"></span><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r861714446"/></span>\n</li>\n<li id="cite_note-102"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a
